        $('.inlinebarrisk-1').sparkline('html', { width: '136px', fillColor: '#00FF00', lineColor: '#888888', height: '24px' });
        $('.inlinebarrisk-2').sparkline('html', { width: '136px', fillColor: '#AAF042', lineColor: '#888888', height: '24px' });

        $('#lnkCalc').click(function () {


            var sha256C = $('#sha256Check:checked').val();

            if (sha256C == undefined) {
                sha256C = false;
            }

            var scryptC = $('#scryptCheck:checked').val();

            if (scryptC == undefined) {
                scryptC = false;
            }

            var url = "/cryptocurrency/?sha256hr=" + $('#sha256HashRate').val() +
                      "&sha256p=" + $('#sha256Power').val() +
                      "&sha256pc=" + $('#sha256PowerCost').val() +
                      "&scrypthr=" + $('#scryptHashRate').val() +
                      "&scryptp=" + $('#scryptPower').val() +
                      "&scryptpc=" + $('#scryptPowerCost').val() +
                      "&scryptnhr=" + $('#scryptNHashRate').val() +
                      "&scryptnp=" + $('#scryptNPower').val() +
                      "&scryptnpc=" + $('#scryptNPowerCost').val() +
                      "&sha256c=" + sha256C +
                      "&scryptc=" + scryptC +
                      "&e=" + $('#e').val();
            $(this).attr('href', url);
        });

        $("[rel='tooltip']").tooltip();
